    function GetCuff()
        local CuffInBackpack = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Cuffing", true)
        local CuffInCharacter = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Cuffing", true)
        return CuffInBackpack and CuffInBackpack.Parent or (CuffInCharacter and CuffInCharacter.Parent or false)
    end
    function SendNotify(NotificationTitle, NotificationText, NotificationDuration)
        Game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
            Title = NotificationTitle,
            Text = NotificationText,
            Duration = NotificationDuration
        })
        local NotificationSound = Instance.New("Sound", Game.Workspace)
        NotificationSound.SoundId = "rbxassetid://3398620867"
        NotificationSound.Volume = 10
        NotificationSound.Ended:Connect(function()
            NotificationSound:Destroy()
        end)
        local SoundInstance = NotificationSound
        NotificationSound.Play(SoundInstance)
    end
    function GetBomb(TargetPlayer)
        local CharacterItemsIterator, CharacterChildIterator, CharacterChildIndex = Ipairs(TargetPlayer.Character:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local CharacterChild
            CharacterChildIndex, CharacterChild = CharacterItemsIterator(CharacterChildIterator, CharacterChildIndex)
            if CharacterChildIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if CharacterChild:IsA("Tool") and CharacterChild.Name == "Bomb" then
                return CharacterChild
            end
        end
        local BackpackChildIterator, BackpackChildIteratorState, BackpackChildIndex = Ipairs(TargetPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local BombTool
            BackpackChildIndex, BombTool = BackpackChildIterator(BackpackChildIteratorState, BackpackChildIndex)
            if BackpackChildIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if BombTool:IsA("Tool") and BombTool.Name == "Bomb" then
                return BombTool
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    function GetDistanceFar(TargetPart)
        return (Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - TargetPart.Position).Magnitude
    end
    function GetNearPlayers(ReferencePlayer, MaxDistance)
        local PlayersService = Game:GetService("Players")
        local NearbyPlayers = {}
        local PlayerCharacter = ReferencePlayer.Character
        if not PlayerCharacter then
            return NearbyPlayers
        end
        local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
        if not HumanoidRootPart then
            return NearbyPlayers
        end
        local PlayerIterator, PlayersList, Index = Ipairs(PlayersService:GetPlayers())
        while true do
            local OtherPlayer
            Index, OtherPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayersList, Index)
            if Index == nil then
                break
            end
            if OtherPlayer ~= ReferencePlayer then
                local PlayerCharacter = OtherPlayer.Character
                if PlayerCharacter then
                    local HumanoidRootPart = PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if HumanoidRootPart then
                        local DistanceToPlayer = (HumanoidRootPart.Position - HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude
                        if DistanceToPlayer <= MaxDistance then
                            Table.Insert(NearbyPlayers, {
                                Player = OtherPlayer,
                                Distance = DistanceToPlayer
                            })
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        Table.Sort(NearbyPlayers, function(FirstPlayerEntry, SecondPlayerEntry)
            return FirstPlayerEntry.Distance < SecondPlayerEntry.Distance
        end)
        local PlayerIterator, PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer = Ipairs(NearbyPlayers)
        local NearPlayersList = {}
        while true do
            local PlayerInstance
            CurrentPlayer, PlayerInstance = PlayerIterator(PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer)
            if CurrentPlayer == nil then
                break
            end
            Table.Insert(NearPlayersList, PlayerInstance.Player)
        end
        return NearPlayersList
    end
    function Send(MessageToSend)
        IsLegacyChat = Game:GetService("TextChatService").ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.LegacyChatService
        if IsLegacyChat then
            Game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").DefaultChatSystemChatEvents.SayMessageRequest:FireServer(Tostring(MessageToSend), "All")
        else
            Game:GetService("TextChatService").TextChannels.RBXGeneral:SendAsync(Tostring(MessageToSend))
        end
    end
    function GetRank()
        if Game:GetService("StarterGui"):FindFirstChild("HDAdminInterface") and Game:GetService("StarterGui").HDAdminInterface.Enabled then
            local RankNameText = Game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.HDAdminInterface.MainFrame.Pages.About.Info.M2RankName.Text
            if RankNameText:Sub(1, 1) == "\'" and RankNameText:Sub(- 1) == "\'" then
                return RankNameText:Sub(2, - 2)
            end
        end
        return "Not Enabled"
    end
    function GetUserPic(UserId)
        return Game:HttpGet("https://thumbnails.roblox.com/v1/users/avatar?userIds=" .. UserId .. "&size=420x420&format=Png&isCircular=false"):Match("\"imageUrl\"%s*:%s*\"([^\"]+)\"")
    end
    function CheckHWID()
        local IteratorFunction, HwidList, CurrentHwid = Ipairs({
            "57D3220E-B408-47A3-95B4-4B8063EC7EAD",
            "d5856005-51ea-496b-8e03-74ee7f287942",
            "2f0d1097-a47b-426d-80d6-618c7b2015fd"
        })
        while true do
            local ClientId
            CurrentHwid, ClientId = IteratorFunction(HwidList, CurrentHwid)
            if CurrentHwid == nil then
                break
            end
            if Game:GetService("RbxAnalyticsService"):GetClientId() == ClientId then
                return {
                    Value = true,
                    ClientId = ClientId
                }
            end
        end
        return {
            Value = false,
            ClientId = nil
        }
    end
    function GetDevice()
        return Table.Find({
            Enum.Platform.IOS,
            Enum.Platform.Android
        }, Game:GetService("UserInputService"):GetPlatform()) and "Mobile" or "PC"
    end
    function Execute(CommandName)
        if GetRank() and GetRank() ~= "Not Enabled" then
            Game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("HDAdminHDClient"):WaitForChild("Signals"):WaitForChild("RequestCommandSilent"):InvokeServer(CommandName)
            SendNotify("System VR7", "Executed " .. Command, 5)
        else
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\217\132\216\167\216\179\217\129 \216\167\217\132\217\133\216\167\216\168 \216\186\217\138\216\177 \217\133\216\175\216\185\217\136\217\133", 5)
        end
    end
    function RandomChar()
        local RandomChars = {}
        for CharIndex = 1, Math.Random(1, 5) do
            RandomChars[CharIndex] = String.Char(Math.Random(32, 126))
        end
        return Table.Concat(RandomChars)
    end
    function GetSofa()
        local BackpackIterator, BackpackState, ToolIndex = Ipairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local ToolInstance
            ToolIndex, ToolInstance = BackpackIterator(BackpackState, ToolIndex)
            if ToolIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if ToolInstance:IsA("Tool") and ToolInstance.Name == "Couch" then
                ToolInstance.Parent = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                return ToolInstance
            end
        end
        local CharacterIterator, CharacterChildren, CharacterIndex = Ipairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local CouchTool
            CharacterIndex, CouchTool = CharacterIterator(CharacterChildren, CharacterIndex)
            if CharacterIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if CouchTool:IsA("Tool") and CouchTool.Name == "Couch" then
                return CouchTool
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    function BrookBring(TargetPlayerName, ShouldTeleportToPlayer)
        local TargetPlayer = Game.Players[TargetPlayerName]
        local PlatformPart
        if Game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Platform") then
            PlatformPart = Game.Workspace:FindFirstChild("Platform")
        else
            PlatformPart = Instance.New("Part", Workspace)
            PlatformPart.Name = "Platform"
            PlatformPart.Anchored = true
            PlatformPart.Size = Vector3.New(200, 1, 200)
            PlatformPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(0, - 500, 0)
            PlatformPart.CanCollide = true
            PlatformPart.Transparency = 1
        end
        local OriginalCFrame = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
        local LoopCounter = 0
        local SineWaveCounter = 0
        while true do
            Task.Wait()
            LoopCounter = LoopCounter + 1
            local SofaInstance = GetSofa()
            if not SofaInstance then
                SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\173\216\170\216\167\216\172 \217\131\217\134\216\168\216\169 \216\173\216\170\216\167 \216\170\217\130\216\175\216\177 \216\170\216\179\216\173\216\168", 5)
                break
            end
            local TargetSeat = nil
            if SofaInstance.Seat1.Occupant ~= nil then
                if SofaInstance.Seat1.Occupant and SofaInstance.Seat1.Occupant == TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid then
                    TargetSeat = SofaInstance.Seat1
                elseif SofaInstance.Seat1.Occupant and SofaInstance.Seat1.Occupant ~= TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid then
                    if SofaInstance.Seat2.Occupant ~= nil then
                        if SofaInstance.Seat2.Occupant and SofaInstance.Seat2.Occupant == TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid then
                            TargetSeat = SofaInstance.Seat2
                        end
                    else
                        TargetSeat = SofaInstance.Seat2
                    end
                end
            else
                TargetSeat = SofaInstance.Seat1
            end
            if TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit and TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.SeatPart == TargetSeat then
                if ShouldTeleportToPlayer then
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState("GettingUp")
                else
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlatformPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 5, 0)
                end
                Wait(1)
                SofaInstance.Parent = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack
                break
            end
            if TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit and TargetPlayer.Character.Humanoid.SeatPart ~= TargetSeat then
                SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\167\217\138\217\133\217\131\217\134 \216\179\216\173\216\168 \216\167\217\132\216\182\216\173\217\138\216\169 \217\132\216\167\217\134\217\135 \217\130\216\167\216\185\216\175", 5)
                break
            end
            if SofaInstance.Parent ~= Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character then
                SofaInstance.Parent = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
            end
            local SineOffset = Math.Sin(SineWaveCounter) * 4
            SineWaveCounter = SineWaveCounter + 0.2
            local TargetPosition = TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position + Vector3.New(0, - 4.5 + SineOffset, 0) + TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * - 0.7 + TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity * Vector3.New(0.2, 0, 0.2)
            local LookDirectionUnit = (TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * Vector3.New(1, 0, 1)).Unit
            TargetSeat.CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetPosition, TargetPosition - LookDirectionUnit)
            if LoopCounter >= 200 then
                break
            end
        end
        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState("GettingUp")
    end
    function ChangeToggleColor(ToggleButton)
        Led = ToggleButton.Ticket_Asset
        if Led.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0) then
            Led.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
        else
            Led.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0)
        end
    end
    function GetPing()
        return Game:GetService("Stats").Network.ServerStatsItem["Data Ping"]:GetValue() / 1000
    end
    local function FindPlayerByName(PlayerNameInput)
        if PlayerNameInput == "" then
            return nil
        end
        local TrimmedInput = PlayerNameInput:Match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
        local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, PlayerIndex = Ipairs(Game.Players:GetPlayers())
        while true do
            local PlayerInstance
            PlayerIndex, PlayerInstance = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, PlayerIndex)
            if PlayerIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if PlayerInstance ~= Game.Players.LocalPlayer then
                local PlayerNameLower = PlayerInstance.Name:Lower():Match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                local DisplayNameLower = PlayerInstance.DisplayName:Lower():Match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
                if PlayerNameLower:Sub(1, # TrimmedInput) == TrimmedInput:Lower() or DisplayNameLower:Sub(1, # TrimmedInput) == TrimmedInput:Lower() then
                    return PlayerInstance
                end
            end
        end
        return nil
    end
    local function IsValidPlayerName(PlayerNameInput)
        if PlayerNameInput == "" then
            return nil
        else
            local CleanedPlayerName = PlayerNameInput:Lower():Match("^%s*(.-)%s*$")
            local LocalPlayer = Game.Players.LocalPlayer
            if LocalPlayer.Name:Lower():Sub(1, # CleanedPlayerName) == CleanedPlayerName or LocalPlayer.DisplayName:Lower():Sub(1, # CleanedPlayerName) == CleanedPlayerName then
                return LocalPlayer
            else
                return nil
            end
        end
    end
    function GetCharacter(PlayerInstance)
        if PlayerInstance.Character then
            return PlayerInstance.Character
        end
    end
    function GetRoot(Player)
        if GetCharacter(Player):FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
            return GetCharacter(Player).HumanoidRootPart
        end
    end
    function TeleportTO(TargetX, TargetY, TargetZ, TargetPlayer, TeleportMode)
        Pcall(function()
            if TeleportMode ~= "safe" then
                GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0, 0)
                if TargetPlayer ~= "pos" then
                    GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(GetRoot(TargetPlayer).Position) + Vector3.New(0, 2, 0)
                else
                    GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetX, TargetY, TargetZ)
                end
            else
                Task.Spawn(function()
                    for _ = 1, 30 do
                        Task.Wait()
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0, 0)
                        if TargetPlayer ~= "pos" then
                            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(GetRoot(TargetPlayer).Position) + Vector3.New(0, 2, 0)
                        else
                            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetX, TargetY, TargetZ)
                        end
                    end
                end)
            end
        end)
    end
    local function IsRootPartValid()
        if RootPart then
            local NextPlayerIterator = Next
            local PlayersList, CurrentPlayer = PlayersService:GetPlayers()
            while true do
                local PlayerInstance
                CurrentPlayer, PlayerInstance = NextPlayerIterator(PlayersList, CurrentPlayer)
                if CurrentPlayer == nil then
                    break
                end
                if PlayerInstance ~= LocalPlayer then
                    local CharacterOrHumanoid = PlayerInstance.Character
                    if CharacterOrHumanoid then
                        CharacterOrHumanoid = CharacterOrHumanoid:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                    end
                    local RootPartOrCharacter
                    if CharacterOrHumanoid then
                        RootPartOrCharacter = CharacterOrHumanoid.RootPart
                    else
                        RootPartOrCharacter = CharacterOrHumanoid
                    end
                    if RootPartOrCharacter and (RootPart.Position - RootPartOrCharacter.Position).Magnitude < 2 then
                        local NextFunction = Next
                        local AnimationTracksIterator, CurrentTrack = CharacterOrHumanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
                        while true do
                            local TrackValue
                            CurrentTrack, TrackValue = NextFunction(AnimationTracksIterator, CurrentTrack)
                            if CurrentTrack == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if TrackValue.Animation and TrackValue.Animation.AnimationId:Match("148840371") or TrackValue.Animation.AnimationId:Match("5918726674") then
                                return true
                            end
                        end
                        return false
                    end
                end
            end
        end
        return false
    end
    function PredictionTP(TargetCharacter, TargetCharacter)
        local TargetRootPart = GetRoot(TargetCharacter)
        local TargetPosition = TargetRootPart.Position
        local TargetVelocity = TargetRootPart.Velocity
        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetPosition.X + TargetVelocity.X * (GetPing() * 3.5), TargetPosition.Y + TargetVelocity.Y * (GetPing() * 2), TargetPosition.Z + TargetVelocity.Z * (GetPing() * 3.5))
        if TargetCharacter == "safe" then
            Task.Wait()
            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetPosition)
            Task.Wait()
            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetPosition.X + TargetVelocity.X * (GetPing() * 3.5), TargetPosition.Y + TargetVelocity.Y * (GetPing() * 2), TargetPosition.Z + TargetVelocity.Z * (GetPing() * 3.5))
        end
    end
    function Cuffbring()
        if Getgenv().Cuff.Bring then
            local CuffedTool = GetCuff()
            if not CuffedTool then
                Game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                    Title = "System VR7",
                    Text = "\239\191\189\216\167\216\178\217\133 \217\138\217\131\217\136\217\134 \217\133\216\185\217\131 \217\131\217\132\216\168\216\180\216\169",
                    Duration = 5
                })
                return
            end
            local PlayerDeathTimes = {}
            local PlayerConnections = {}
            local function HandlePlayerAdded(Player)
                local function TrackPlayerCharacter(Character)
                    local Humanoid = Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
                    if Humanoid then
                        local DeathConnection = Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                            PlayerDeathTimes[Player] = Os.Time()
                        end)
                        Table.Insert(PlayerConnections, DeathConnection)
                    end
                end
                if Player.Character then
                    TrackPlayerCharacter(Player.Character)
                end
                local CharacterAddedConnection = Player.CharacterAdded:Connect(TrackPlayerCharacter)
                Table.Insert(PlayerConnections, CharacterAddedConnection)
            end
            local PlayerIterator, PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer = Ipairs(Game.Players:GetPlayers())
            local PlayerConnections = PlayerDeathTimes
            local ConnectionList = PlayerConnections
            while true do
                local PlayerOrNil
                CurrentPlayer, PlayerOrNil = PlayerIterator(PlayerIndex, CurrentPlayer)
                if CurrentPlayer == nil then
                    break
                end
                HandlePlayerAdded(PlayerOrNil)
            end
            local PlayerAddedConnection = Game.Players.PlayerAdded:Connect(HandlePlayerAdded)
            Table.Insert(ConnectionList, PlayerAddedConnection)
            Task.Spawn(function()
                if Getgenv().Cuff.Throw then
                    local OriginalCFrame = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    while Getgenv().Cuff.Throw do
                        Wait()
                        Pcall(function()
                            Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(0, 1000000, 0) * CFrame.Angles(Math.Rad(- 90), 0, 0)
                            Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.New()
                            Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = true
                        end)
                    end
                    Pcall(function()
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                    end)
                end
            end)
            while Getgenv().Cuff.Bring do
                Wait()
                local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, CurrentIndex = Ipairs(Game.Players:GetPlayers())
                while true do
                    local TargetPlayer
                    CurrentIndex, TargetPlayer = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, CurrentIndex)
                    if CurrentIndex == nil or not Getgenv().Cuff.Bring then
                        break
                    end
                    if TargetPlayer ~= Game.Players.LocalPlayer and TargetPlayer.Character and (not TargetPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("ForceField") and (not PlayerConnections[TargetPlayer] or Os.Time() - PlayerConnections[TargetPlayer] > 8)) then
                        Pcall(function()
                            if CuffedTool and CuffedTool.Parent == Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack then
                                CuffedTool.Parent = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character
                            end
                            CuffedTool.RemoteEvent:FireServer(TargetPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart, "Cuff")
                            Task.Wait(0.3)
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
            local IteratorFunction, PlayerList, Index = Ipairs(ConnectionList)
            while true do
                local Connection
                Index, Connection = IteratorFunction(PlayerList, Index)
                if Index == nil then
                    break
                end
                if Connection and Connection.Connected then
                    Connection:Disconnect()
                end
            end
        end
    end

    function WhatTime()
        return Os.Date("*t").Hour >= 12 and "dark" or "light"
    end
    function PlayAnim(AnimationId, TimePosition, PlaybackSpeed, DisableAnimate)
        local ShouldDisableAnimate = DisableAnimate
        Pcall(function()
            if not ShouldDisableAnimate then
                LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
            end
            local Humanoid = LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid
            local PlayingAnimationTracks = Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
            local AnimationTrackIterator, AnimationTrackTable, AnimationTrackKey = Pairs(PlayingAnimationTracks)
            while true do
                local CurrentAnimationTrack
                AnimationTrackKey, CurrentAnimationTrack = AnimationTrackIterator(AnimationTrackTable, AnimationTrackKey)
                if AnimationTrackKey == nil then
                    break
                end
                CurrentAnimationTrack:Stop()
            end
            LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = true
            local AnimationInstance = Instance.New("Animation")
            AnimationInstance.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://" .. AnimationId
            local AnimationTrack = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(AnimationInstance)
            AnimationTrack:Play()
            AnimationTrack.TimePosition = TimePosition
            AnimationTrack:AdjustSpeed(PlaybackSpeed)
            AnimationTrack.Stopped:Connect(function()
                LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
                local PairsIterator, AnimationTable, TrackName = Pairs(PlayingAnimationTracks)
                while true do
                    local AnimationTrack
                    TrackName, AnimationTrack = PairsIterator(AnimationTable, TrackName)
                    if TrackName == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    AnimationTrack:Stop()
                end
                AnimationInstance:Destroy()
            end)
        end)
    end
    function StopAnim()
        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Animate.Disabled = false
        local PlayingTracks = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
        local TrackIterator, TrackTable, AnimationTrack = Pairs(PlayingTracks)
        while true do
            local CurrentAnimationTrack
            AnimationTrack, CurrentAnimationTrack = TrackIterator(TrackTable, AnimationTrack)
            if AnimationTrack == nil then
                break
            end
            CurrentAnimationTrack:Stop()
        end
        Wait(0.1)
    end
    function CheckAnim(TargetAnimationId)
        local PlayingAnimationTracks = LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks()
        local AnimationTrackIterator, AnimationTrackState, AnimationTrack = Pairs(PlayingAnimationTracks)
        while true do
            local AnimationTrackInfo
            AnimationTrack, AnimationTrackInfo = AnimationTrackIterator(AnimationTrackState, AnimationTrack)
            if AnimationTrack == nil then
                break
            end
            local AnimationIdNumber = AnimationTrackInfo.Animation.AnimationId:Match("%d+")
            if Tonumber(AnimationIdNumber) == Tonumber(TargetAnimationId) then
                return true
            end
        end
        return false
    end

    function CreateRainbowTextLabel(ParentFrame, TextContent, LabelPosition, LabelRotation)
        local RainbowTextLabel = Instance.New("TextLabel", ParentFrame)
        RainbowTextLabel.Text = TextContent
        RainbowTextLabel.Size = UDim2.New(0, 60, 0, 30)
        RainbowTextLabel.Position = LabelPosition
        RainbowTextLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(85, 255, 127)
        RainbowTextLabel.TextScaled = true
        RainbowTextLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSans
        RainbowTextLabel.TextSize = 20
        RainbowTextLabel.TextTransparency = 0
        RainbowTextLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        RainbowTextLabel.TextStrokeTransparency = 0.8
        RainbowTextLabel.TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        RainbowTextLabel.Rotation = LabelRotation
        return RainbowTextLabel
    end
    function CreateButtonWithText(ParentFrame, ButtonName, ButtonText, ButtonPosition, ButtonText, TextColor)
        local ButtonInstance = Instance.New("TextButton", ParentFrame)
        ButtonInstance.Name = ButtonName
        ButtonInstance.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(PrimaryColorR, GreenComponent, BlueComponent)
        ButtonInstance.BackgroundTransparency = 0.5
        ButtonInstance.BorderColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        ButtonInstance.BorderSizePixel = 0
        ButtonInstance.Position = ButtonPosition
        ButtonInstance.Size = UDim2.New(0, 150, 0, 30)
        ButtonInstance.Font = Enum.Font.Oswald
        ButtonInstance.Text = ButtonText
        ButtonInstance.TextColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        ButtonInstance.TextScaled = true
        ButtonInstance.TextSize = 14
        ButtonInstance.TextWrapped = true
        if ButtonName == "VehicleFling_Button" or (ButtonName == "Ball_Fling" or (ButtonName == "Spam_Skins" or ButtonName == "Spamming_Commands")) then
            CreateToggle(ButtonInstance)
        else
            CreateClicker(ButtonInstance)
        end
        return {
            RainbowTextLabel = CreateRainbowTextLabel(ParentFrame, ButtonText, UDim2.New(0, ButtonPosition.X.Offset - 15, 0, ButtonPosition.Y.Offset + 15), TextColor),
            ToggleButton = ButtonInstance
        }
    end
    if game.PlaceId == 14201103742 or (game.PlaceId == 12123568130 or (game.PlaceId == 18209796679 or game.PlaceId == 17723040340)) then
        pcall(function()
            local Workspace = Game:GetService("Workspace")
            local RunService = Game:GetService("RunService")
            local LocalPlayer = Game.Players.LocalPlayer
            local HumanoidRootPart = (LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()):WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
            local FlingFolder = Instance.New("Folder", Workspace)
            local FlingPart = Instance.New("Part", FlingFolder)
            local FlingAttachment = Instance.New("Attachment", FlingPart)
            FlingPart.Anchored = true
            FlingPart.CanCollide = false
            FlingPart.Transparency = 1
            if not Getgenv().Network then
                Getgenv().Network = {
                    BaseParts = {},
                    Velocity = Vector3.New(14.46262424, 14.46262424, 14.46262424)
                }
                function Network.RetainPart(RetainedPart)
                    if Typeof(RetainedPart) == "Instance" and (RetainedPart:IsA("BasePart") and (RetainedPart:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) and not RetainedPart:IsDescendantOf(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character))) then
                        Table.Insert(Network.BaseParts, RetainedPart)
                        RetainedPart.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.New(0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
                        RetainedPart.CanCollide = false
                    end
                end;
                (function()
                    LocalPlayer.ReplicationFocus = Workspace
                    RunService.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
                        Pcall(function()
                            Sethiddenproperty(LocalPlayer, "SimulationRadius", Math.Huge)
                            local BasePartsIterator, BasePartsTable, CurrentBasePart = Pairs(Network.BaseParts)
                            while true do
                                local BasePartInstance
                                CurrentBasePart, BasePartInstance = BasePartsIterator(BasePartsTable, CurrentBasePart)
                                if CurrentBasePart == nil then
                                    break
                                end
                                if BasePartInstance:IsDescendantOf(Workspace) then
                                    BasePartInstance.Velocity = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.LookVector * 50
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                    end)
                end)()
            end
            function Flinger(TargetPart)
                if Getgenv().Loopfling and (TargetPart:IsA("BasePart") and not TargetPart.Anchored) and (not TargetPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (not TargetPart.Parent:FindFirstChild("Head") and TargetPart.Name ~= "Handle")) then
                    local OriginalCFrame = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(TargetPart.Position)
                    Wait(0.7)
                    local NextFunction = Next
                    local ChildObjects, CurrentChild = TargetPart:GetChildren()
                    while true do
                        local ChildInstance
                        CurrentChild, ChildInstance = NextFunction(ChildObjects, CurrentChild)
                        if CurrentChild == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if ChildInstance:IsA("BodyAngularVelocity") or (ChildInstance:IsA("BodyForce") or (ChildInstance:IsA("BodyGyro") or (ChildInstance:IsA("BodyPosition") or (ChildInstance:IsA("BodyThrust") or (ChildInstance:IsA("BodyVelocity") or ChildInstance:IsA("RocketPropulsion")))))) then
                            ChildInstance:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                    if TargetPart:FindFirstChild("Attachment") then
                        TargetPart:FindFirstChild("Attachment"):Destroy()
                    end
                    if TargetPart:FindFirstChild("AlignPosition") then
                        TargetPart:FindFirstChild("AlignPosition"):Destroy()
                    end
                    if TargetPart:FindFirstChild("Torque") then
                        TargetPart:FindFirstChild("Torque"):Destroy()
                    end
                    TargetPart.CustomPhysicalProperties = PhysicalProperties.New(0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
                    TargetPart.CanCollide = false
                    TargetPart.CanTouch = false
                    local AntiFlingTorque = Instance.New("Torque", TargetPart)
                    AntiFlingTorque.Torque = Vector3.New(100000, 100000, 100000)
                    local AlignPositionInstance = Instance.New("AlignPosition", TargetPart)
                    local AttachmentInstance = Instance.New("Attachment", TargetPart)
                    AntiFlingTorque.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
                    AlignPositionInstance.MaxForce = 1e17
                    AlignPositionInstance.MaxVelocity = Math.Huge
                    AlignPositionInstance.Responsiveness = 200
                    AlignPositionInstance.Attachment0 = AttachmentInstance
                    AlignPositionInstance.Attachment1 = FlingAttachment
                    Spawn(function()
                        while true do
                            Task.Wait()
                            if Getgenv().Loopfling then
                                Pcall(function()
                                    if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health ~= 0 then
                                        Getgenv().Look = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame + Vector3.New(0, - 1, 0)
                                    end
                                end)
                            end
                            if Getgenv().Ejnfja then
                                return
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    Spawn(function()
                        TargetPart.CFrame = HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        if Getgenv().Working then
                            return
                        else
                            local RotationAngle = 0
                            while true do
                                Getgenv().Working = true
                                Task.Wait()
                                Pcall(function()
                                    RotationAngle = RotationAngle + Math.Rad(60)
                                    local OffsetCFrame = CFrame.New(Math.Sin(RotationAngle) * 3, 0, Math.Cos(RotationAngle) * 3)
                                    FlingAttachment.WorldCFrame = Getgenv().Look * OffsetCFrame
                                    TargetPart.CFrame = Getgenv().Look * OffsetCFrame
                                    TargetPart.Velocity = Getgenv().Look.LookVector * 10000
                                end)
                            end
                        end
                    end)
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalCFrame
                end
            end
        end)
    end

    task.wait(0.5)
    function ChangeSection(SectionButton)
        SectionClickedName = String.Split(SectionButton.Name, "_")[1]
        local SectionsContainer = SectionList
        local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, CurrentChild = Pairs(SectionsContainer:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local ChildInstance
            CurrentChild, ChildInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, CurrentChild)
            if CurrentChild == nil then
                break
            end
            if ChildInstance.Name == SectionButton.Name then
                ChildInstance.Transparency = 0
            else
                ChildInstance.Transparency = 0.5
            end
        end
        local ChildrenContainer = BackgroundImageLabel
        local ChildIterator, ChildTable, CurrentChild = Pairs(ChildrenContainer:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local SectionFrame
            CurrentChild, SectionFrame = ChildIterator(ChildTable, CurrentChild)
            if CurrentChild == nil then
                break
            end
            if SectionFrame:IsA("ScrollingFrame") then
                SectionForName = String.Split(SectionFrame.Name, "_")[1]
                if String.Find(SectionClickedName, SectionForName) then
                    SectionFrame.Visible = true
                else
                    SectionFrame.Visible = false
                end
            end
        end
    end

    function UpdateTarget(TargetPlayer)
        Pcall(function()
            if Table.Find(BannedUserIds, Tostring(TargetPlayer.UserId)) or (Table.Find(Loadstring(Game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Hm5011/hussain/refs/heads/main/Hehehe"))(), Tostring(TargetPlayer.UserId)) or Table.Find(Loadstring(Game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/VR7ss/OMK/refs/heads/main/Usernames"))(), Tostring(TargetPlayer.UserId))) then
                Game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                    Title = "VR7 Team",
                    Text = "\239\191\189\216\167\217\138\217\133\217\131\217\134\217\131 \216\167\216\174\216\170\217\138\216\167\216\177 \217\135\216\176\216\167 \216\167\217\132\216\167\216\185\216\168\n \217\132\216\167\217\134\217\135 \217\133\216\173\217\133\217\138 \217\133\217\134 \216\181\216\167\216\173\216\168 \216\167\217\132\216\179\217\131\216\177\216\168\216\170",
                    Duration = 5,
                    Icon = "rbxassetid://136772242182146"
                })
                local SoundEffect = Instance.New("Sound", Game.Workspace)
                SoundEffect.SoundId = "rbxassetid://1862047553"
                SoundEffect.Volume = 10
                SoundEffect.Ended:Connect(function()
                    SoundEffect:Destroy()

    WalkSpeedButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if Game.PlaceId ~= 11379739543 then

            end)
        else
            if Getgenv().Tpwalking then
                Getgenv().Tpwalking = false
                SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\182\216\186\216\183 \217\133\216\177\216\169 \216\171\216\167\217\134\217\138\216\169 \217\132\217\132\216\170\216\179\216\177\217\138\216\185", 5)
            elseif not Getgenv().Tpwalking then
                Getgenv().Tpwalking = true
                SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\182\216\186\216\183 \217\133\216\177\216\169 \216\171\216\167\217\134\217\138\216\169 \217\132\216\167\216\177\216\172\216\167\216\185 \216\167\217\132\216\179\216\177\216\185\216\169 \216\167\217\132\216\183\216\168\217\138\216\185\217\138\216\169", 5)
            end
            local JumpPowerText = WalkSpeedInput.Text:Gsub("%D", "")
            local JumpPowerValue = JumpPowerText == "" and 1 or (Tonumber(JumpPowerText) > 10 and 10 or JumpPowerText)
            while Getgenv().Tpwalking do
                Task.Wait()
                Pcall(function()
                    local HeartbeatWaitResult = Game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
                    if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.MoveDirection.Magnitude <= 0 then
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:TranslateBy(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.MoveDirection * HeartbeatWaitResult * 10)

                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:TranslateBy(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.MoveDirection * JumpPowerValue * HeartbeatWaitResult * 10)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end

    local ClonedCharacter = nil
    local PlayerCharacter = nil
    local IsInvisible = nil
    local IsFlinging = nil
    InvisibleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(InvisibleButton)
        if InvisibleButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            Pcall(function()
                if IsFlinging and (PlayerCharacter and ClonedCharacter) and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (ClonedCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (ClonedCharacter.Humanoid.Health > 0 and PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Health))) then
                    Invisible()
                end
            end)
        else
            if not Getgenv().EnabledBefore then
                Getgenv().EnabledBefore = true
                local LocalPlayer = Game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
                PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                IsInvisible = false
                PlayerCharacter.Archivable = true
                ClonedCharacter = PlayerCharacter:Clone()
                local PlatformPart = Instance.New("Part", Workspace)
                PlatformPart.Anchored = true
                PlatformPart.Size = Vector3.New(200, 1, 200)
                PlatformPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(0, - 500, 0)
                PlatformPart.CanCollide = true
                PlatformPart.Transparency = 1
                ClonedCharacter.Parent = Workspace
                ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlatformPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 5, 0)
                local TargetPlayer = PlayerCharacter
                local NextChildIterator, ChildTable, ChildIterator = Pairs(TargetPlayer:GetChildren())
                while true do
                    local ChildInstance
                    ChildIterator, ChildInstance = NextChildIterator(ChildTable, ChildIterator)
                    if ChildIterator == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if ChildInstance:IsA("LocalScript") then
                        local ClonedScript = ChildInstance:Clone()
                        ClonedScript.Disabled = true
                        ClonedScript.Parent = ClonedCharacter
                    end
                end
                local TargetContainer = ClonedCharacter
                local DescendantIterator, CurrentDescendantIterator, CurrentDescendantKey = Pairs(TargetContainer:GetDescendants())
                while true do
                    local CurrentDescendant
                    CurrentDescendantKey, CurrentDescendant = DescendantIterator(CurrentDescendantIterator, CurrentDescendantKey)
                    if CurrentDescendantKey == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if CurrentDescendant:IsA("BasePart") and CurrentDescendant.Name == "HumanoidRootPart" then
                        CurrentDescendant.Transparency = 1
                    elseif CurrentDescendant:IsA("BasePart") then
                        CurrentDescendant.Transparency = 0.5
                    end
                end
                IsFlinging = true
                local function WaitForRootPart()
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    if ClonedCharacter and ClonedCharacter.Parent then
                        ClonedCharacter:Destroy()
                    end
                    if PlatformPart and PlatformPart.Parent then
                        PlatformPart:Destroy()
                    end
                    PlayerCharacter.Archivable = true
                    ClonedCharacter = PlayerCharacter:Clone()
                    PlatformPart = Instance.New("Part", Workspace)
                    PlatformPart.Anchored = true
                    PlatformPart.Size = Vector3.New(200, 1, 200)
                    PlatformPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(0, - 500, 0)
                    PlatformPart.CanCollide = true
                    PlatformPart.Transparency = 1
                    ClonedCharacter.Parent = Workspace
                    ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlatformPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 5, 0)
                    local CharacterModel = ClonedCharacter
                    local IteratorFunction, TableToIterate, CurrentKey = Pairs(CharacterModel:GetChildren())
                    while true do
                        local CurrentValue
                        CurrentKey, CurrentValue = IteratorFunction(TableToIterate, CurrentKey)
                        if CurrentKey == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if CurrentValue:IsA("LocalScript") then
                            local ClonedScript = CurrentValue:Clone()
                            ClonedScript.Disabled = true
                            ClonedScript.Parent = ClonedCharacter
                        end
                    end
                    local Descendants = ClonedCharacter
                    local IteratorFunction, DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex = Pairs(Descendants:GetDescendants())
                    while true do
                        local CurrentInstance
                        CurrentIndex, CurrentInstance = IteratorFunction(DescendantsTable, CurrentIndex)
                        if CurrentIndex == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if CurrentInstance:IsA("BasePart") then
                            if CurrentInstance.Name ~= "HumanoidRootPart" then
                                CurrentInstance.Transparency = 0.5
                            else
                                CurrentInstance.Transparency = 1
                            end
                        end
                    end
                    if ClonedCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                        ClonedCharacter.Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                            if PlayerCharacter and PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
                                PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Health = 0
                            end
                        end)
                    end
                    PseudoAnchor = ClonedCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                end
                function CharacterDied()
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart")
                    IsFlinging = false
                    LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    PlayerCharacter = LocalPlayer.Character or LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:Wait()
                    IsFlinging = true
                    IsInvisible = false
                    local Character = PlayerCharacter
                    Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
                    PlayerCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Died:Connect(function()
                        CharacterDied()
                        InvisibleButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                    end)
                    WaitForRootPart()
                end
                PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                    ClonedCharacter:Destroy()
                end)
                ClonedCharacter.Humanoid.Died:Connect(function()
                    PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Health = 0
                end)
                LocalPlayer.CharacterAppearanceLoaded:Connect(CharacterDied)
                local TargetRootPart = nil
                Game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                    if TargetRootPart ~= nil then
                        TargetRootPart.CFrame = PlatformPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 5, 0)
                    end
                end)
                TargetRootPart = ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart
                function Invisible()
                    if IsInvisible then
                        local OriginalCameraCFrame = Workspace.Camera.CFrame
                        local PlayerRootPartCFrame = ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlayerRootPartCFrame
                        ClonedCharacter.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
                        LocalPlayer.Character = PlayerCharacter
                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = PlayerCharacter.Humanoid
                        TargetRootPart = ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart
                        local CharacterInstance = ClonedCharacter
                        local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, CurrentIndex = Pairs(CharacterInstance:GetChildren())
                        while true do
                            local CurrentChild
                            CurrentIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, CurrentIndex)
                            if CurrentIndex == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if CurrentChild:IsA("LocalScript") then
                                CurrentChild.Disabled = true
                            end
                        end
                        Task.Wait()
                        Workspace.Camera.CFrame = OriginalCameraCFrame
                        IsInvisible = false
                        InvisibleButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                    else
                        local OriginalCameraCFrame = Workspace.Camera.CFrame
                        local OriginalRootCFrame = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
                        PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = PlatformPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 5, 0)
                        Task.Wait(0.1)
                        ClonedCharacter.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = OriginalRootCFrame
                        PlayerCharacter.Humanoid:UnequipTools()
                        LocalPlayer.Character = ClonedCharacter
                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = ClonedCharacter.Humanoid
                        TargetRootPart = PlayerCharacter.HumanoidRootPart
                        local TargetPlayer = ClonedCharacter
                        local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, CurrentIndex = Pairs(TargetPlayer:GetChildren())
                        while true do
                            local ScriptInstance
                            CurrentIndex, ScriptInstance = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, CurrentIndex)
                            if CurrentIndex == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if ScriptInstance:IsA("LocalScript") then
                                ScriptInstance.Disabled = false
                            end
                        end
                        Task.Wait()
                        Workspace.Camera.CFrame = OriginalCameraCFrame
                        IsInvisible = true
                        InvisibleButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0)
                    end
                end
                WaitForRootPart()
                PlayerCharacter:WaitForChild("Humanoid").Died:Connect(function()
                    CharacterDied()
                end)
            end
            Pcall(function()
                if IsFlinging and (PlayerCharacter and ClonedCharacter) and (PlayerCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (ClonedCharacter:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (ClonedCharacter.Humanoid.Health > 0 and PlayerCharacter.Humanoid.Health))) then
                    Invisible()
                end
            end)
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\176\216\167 \217\133\216\170\216\170 \216\180\216\186\217\132 \216\167\217\132\216\167\216\174\216\170\217\129\216\167\216\161 \217\133\217\134 \216\172\216\175\217\138\216\175", 5)
        end
    end)
    ShiftLockButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(ShiftLockButton)
        if ShiftLockButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            if Game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ShiftlockGui") then
                Game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ShiftlockGui").Enabled = false
                Game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ShiftlockGui").LockButton.BtnIcon.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                EndForceShiftLock()
            end
        else
            if Game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ShiftlockGui") then
                Game.CoreGui:FindFirstChild("ShiftlockGui").Enabled = true
                return
            end
            local ShiftlockGui = Instance.New("ScreenGui")
            local LockButton = Instance.New("ImageButton")
            local BtnIcon = Instance.New("ImageLabel")
            local UICorner = Instance.New("UICorner")
            Instance.New("UICorner")
            ShiftlockGui.Name = "ShiftlockGui"
            ShiftlockGui.ZIndexBehavior = Enum.ZIndexBehavior.Sibling
            ShiftlockGui.ResetOnSpawn = false
            ShiftlockGui.DisplayOrder = 69
            ShiftlockGui.Parent = Game.CoreGui
            LockButton.Name = "LockButton"
            LockButton.Parent = ShiftlockGui
            LockButton.AnchorPoint = Vector2.New(0.5, 0.5)
            LockButton.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(0, 0, 255)
            LockButton.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            LockButton.BorderSizePixel = 0
            LockButton.Position = UDim2.New(0.785, 0, 0.865, 0)
            LockButton.Size = UDim2.New(0, 65, 0, 65)
            LockButton.ZIndex = 3
            LockButton.Image = ""
            LockButton.AutoButtonColor = true
            LockButton.Draggable = true
            UICorner.Parent = LockButton
            UICorner.CornerRadius = UDim.New(1, 0)
            BtnIcon.Name = "BtnIcon"
            BtnIcon.Parent = LockButton
            BtnIcon.BackgroundTransparency = 1
            BtnIcon.Position = UDim2.New(0.15, 0, 0.15, 0)
            BtnIcon.Size = UDim2.New(0.7, 0, 0.7, 0)
            BtnIcon.ZIndex = 3
            BtnIcon.Image = "rbxasset://textures/ui/mouseLock_off.png"
            BtnIcon.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            BtnIcon.ScaleType = Enum.ScaleType.Fit
            local function LocalScriptFunction()
                local LocalScript = Instance.New("LocalScript", LockButton)
                Game:GetService("UserInputService")
                local IsButtonToggled = false
                local ButtonInstance = LocalScript.Parent
                ButtonInstance.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
                    IsButtonToggled = not IsButtonToggled
                    if IsButtonToggled then
                        ButtonInstance.BtnIcon.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(0, 170, 255)
                        Spawn(function()
                            while true do
                                if not IsButtonToggled then
                                    return
                                end
                                for _ = 0.3, 0.7, 0.1 do
                                    if not IsButtonToggled then
                                        break
                                    end
                                    Wait(0.1)
                                end
                                for _ = 0.7, 0.3, - 0.1 do
                                    if not IsButtonToggled then
                                        break
                                    end
                                    Wait(0.1)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        ForceShiftLock()
                    else
                        ButtonInstance.BtnIcon.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 255, 255)
                        EndForceShiftLock()
                    end
                end)
                local OriginalRotationType = nil
                local UserGameSettings = UserSettings():GetService("UserGameSettings")
                local RenderSteppedConnection = nil
                function ForceShiftLock()
                    local _, OriginalRotationType = Pcall(function()
                        return UserGameSettings.RotationType
                    end)
                    OriginalRotationType = OriginalRotationType
                    RenderSteppedConnection = Game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                        Pcall(function()
                            UserGameSettings.RotationType = Enum.RotationType.CameraRelative
                        end)
                    end)
                end
                function EndForceShiftLock()
                    if RenderSteppedConnection then
                        RenderSteppedConnection:Disconnect()
                        Pcall(function()
                            UserGameSettings.RotationType = OriginalRotationType or Enum.RotationType.MovementRelative
                        end)
                    end
                end
            end
            Coroutine.Wrap(LocalScriptFunction)()
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\217\133\217\131\217\134\217\131 \216\179\216\173\216\168 \216\167\217\132\216\178\216\177 \217\132\216\167\217\138 \217\133\217\131\216\167\217\134 \216\170\216\177\217\138\216\175\217\135", 3)
        end
    end)

    NoclipButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(NoclipButton)
        if NoclipButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            local IteratorFunction, ChildIndex, ChildInstance = Ipairs(GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Parent:GetChildren())
            local BasePartsList = {}
            while true do
                local CurrentChild
                ChildInstance, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildIndex, ChildInstance)
                if ChildInstance == nil then
                    break
                end
                if CurrentChild:IsA("BasePart") then
                    Table.Insert(BasePartsList, CurrentChild)
                end
            end
            repeat
                Wait(0.1)
                Pcall(function()
                    local IteratorFunction, Table, Index = Ipairs(BasePartsList)
                    while true do
                        local Value
                        Index, Value = IteratorFunction(Table, Index)
                        if Index == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if LocalPlayer.Character[Value.Name].CanCollide then
                            Task.Wait()
                            LocalPlayer.Character[Value.Name].CanCollide = false
                        end
                    end
                end)
            until NoclipButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            local IteratorFunction, ColorIndex, CurrentIndex = Ipairs(BasePartsList)
            while true do
                local PartName
                CurrentIndex, PartName = IteratorFunction(ColorIndex, CurrentIndex)
                if CurrentIndex == nil then
                    break
                end
                if not LocalPlayer.Character[PartName.Name].CanCollide then
                    Task.Wait(0.01)
                    LocalPlayer.Character[PartName.Name].CanCollide = true
                end
            end
            Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState("GettingUp")
        end
    end)
    SaveCheckpointButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        SavedPosition = GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Position
        SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\217\133 \216\173\217\129\216\184 \216\167\217\132\216\180\217\138\217\131 \216\168\217\136\217\138\217\134\216\170", 5)

    ClearCheckpointButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        SavedPosition = nil
        SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\217\133 \216\173\216\176\217\129 \216\167\217\132\216\180\217\138\217\131 \216\168\217\136\217\138\217\134\216\170", 5)
    end)
    local IsToggleEnabled = true
    local MovementInput = {
        ForwardMovement = 0,
        b = 0,
        LeftMovement = 0,
        r = 0
    }
    local FlyVelocitySettings = {
        ForwardMovement = 0,
        b = 0,
        LeftMovement = 0,
        r = 0
    }
    local KeyDownConnection = nil
    local KeyUpConnection = nil
    ToggleButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(ToggleButton)
        if ToggleButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            IsToggleEnabled = false
            FlyPadButton.Visible = false
            KeyDownConnection:Disconnect()
            KeyUpConnection:Disconnect()
            StopAnim()
        else
            IsToggleEnabled = true
            if Game:GetService("UserInputService").TouchEnabled then
                FlyPadButton.Visible = true
            end
            local CharacterTorso = LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso")
            local WalkTime = 0
            local function CreateAntiFlingBodies()
                local BodyGyroInstance = Instance.New("BodyGyro", CharacterTorso)
                BodyGyroInstance.GyroProportionalGain = 90000
                BodyGyroInstance.MaxTorque = Vector3.New(9000000000, 9000000000, 9000000000)
                BodyGyroInstance.Cframe = CharacterTorso.CFrame
                local BodyVelocityInstance = Instance.New("BodyVelocity", CharacterTorso)
                BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0.1, 0)
                BodyVelocityInstance.MaxForce = Vector3.New(9000000000, 9000000000, 9000000000)
                PlayAnim(10714347256, 4, 0)
                while true do
                    Task.Wait()
                    LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true
                    if MovementInput.LeftMovement + MovementInput.r ~= 0 or MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b ~= 0 then
                        WalkTime = WalkTime + SpeedMultiplier * 0.1
                        if SpeedMultiplier < WalkTime then
                            WalkTime = SpeedMultiplier
                        end
                    elseif MovementInput.LeftMovement + MovementInput.r == 0 and (MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b == 0 and WalkTime ~= 0) then
                        WalkTime = WalkTime - SpeedMultiplier * 0.1
                        if WalkTime < 0 then
                            WalkTime = 0
                        end
                    end
                    if MovementInput.LeftMovement + MovementInput.r ~= 0 or MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b ~= 0 then
                        BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = (Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.LookVector * (MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b) + (Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.New(MovementInput.LeftMovement + MovementInput.r, (MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b) * 0.2, 0).Position - Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.Position)) * WalkTime
                        FlyVelocitySettings = {
                            ForwardMovement = MovementInput.ForwardMovement,
                            b = MovementInput.b,
                            LeftMovement = MovementInput.LeftMovement,
                            r = MovementInput.r
                        }
                    elseif MovementInput.LeftMovement + MovementInput.r ~= 0 or (MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b ~= 0 or WalkTime == 0) then
                        BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0.1, 0)
                    else
                        BodyVelocityInstance.Velocity = (Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.LookVector * (FlyVelocitySettings.ForwardMovement + FlyVelocitySettings.b) + (Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.New(FlyVelocitySettings.LeftMovement + FlyVelocitySettings.r, (FlyVelocitySettings.ForwardMovement + FlyVelocitySettings.b) * 0.2, 0).Position - Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.Position)) * WalkTime
                    end
                    BodyGyroInstance.Cframe = Game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.Angles(- Math.Rad((MovementInput.ForwardMovement + MovementInput.b) * 50 * WalkTime / SpeedMultiplier), 0, 0)
                    if not IsToggleEnabled then
                        MovementInput = {
                            ForwardMovement = 0,
                            b = 0,
                            LeftMovement = 0,
                            r = 0
                        }
                        FlyVelocitySettings = {
                            ForwardMovement = 0,
                            b = 0,
                            LeftMovement = 0,
                            r = 0
                        }
                        WalkTime = 0
                        BodyGyroInstance:Destroy()
                        BodyVelocityInstance:Destroy()
                        LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
                        return
                    end
                end
            end
            KeyDownConnection = PlayerMouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(KeyPressed)
                if KeyPressed:Lower() ~= "w" then
                    if KeyPressed:Lower() ~= "s" then
                        if KeyPressed:Lower() ~= "a" then
                            if KeyPressed:Lower() == "d" then
                                MovementInput.r = 1
                                PlayAnim(10147823318, 4.81, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            MovementInput.LeftMovement = - 1
                            PlayAnim(10147823318, 3.55, 0)
                        end
                    else
                        MovementInput.b = - 1
                        PlayAnim(10147823318, 4.11, 0)
                    end
                else
                    MovementInput.ForwardMovement = 1
                    if LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RigType ~= Enum.HumanoidRigType.IsR15RigType then
                        PlayAnim(282574440, 4.65, 0)
                    else
                        PlayAnim(10714177846, 4.65, 0)
                    end
                end
            end)
            KeyUpConnection = PlayerMouse.KeyUp:Connect(function(KeyReleased)
                if KeyReleased:Lower() ~= "w" then
                    if KeyReleased:Lower() ~= "s" then
                        if KeyReleased:Lower() ~= "a" then
                            if KeyReleased:Lower() == "d" then
                                MovementInput.r = 0
                                PlayAnim(10714347256, 4, 0)
                            end
                        else
                            MovementInput.LeftMovement = 0
                            PlayAnim(10714347256, 4, 0)
                        end
                    else
                        MovementInput.b = 0
                        PlayAnim(10714347256, 4, 0)
                    end
                else
                    MovementInput.ForwardMovement = 0
                    PlayAnim(10714347256, 4, 0)
                end
            end)
            CreateAntiFlingBodies()
        end
    end)
