    ClickTargetToolButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local IteratorFunction, IteratorState, BackpackItemIterator = Ipairs(LocalPlayer.Backpack:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local BackpackItem
            BackpackItemIterator, BackpackItem = IteratorFunction(IteratorState, BackpackItemIterator)
            if BackpackItemIterator == nil then
                break
            end
            if BackpackItem.Name == "ClickTarget" then
                BackpackItem:Destroy()
            end
        end
        local CharacterPartIterator, CharacterParts, CharacterPartIndex = Ipairs(LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren())
        while true do
            local TargetPart
            CharacterPartIndex, TargetPart = CharacterPartIterator(CharacterParts, CharacterPartIndex)
            if CharacterPartIndex == nil then
                break
            end
            if TargetPart.Name == "ClickTarget" then
                TargetPart:Destroy()
            end
        end
        local ClickTool = Instance.New("Tool")
        ClickTool.Name = "ClickTarget"
        ClickTool.RequiresHandle = false
        ClickTool.TextureId = "rbxassetid://13769558274"
        ClickTool.ToolTip = "\239\191\189\216\174\216\170\216\167\216\177 \216\180\216\174\216\181"
        local function HandleClickActivation()
            GetRoot(LocalPlayer)
            local RaycastTarget = PlayerMouse.Target
            local TargetPlayer = nil
            if RaycastTarget and RaycastTarget.Parent then
                if RaycastTarget.Parent:IsA("Model") then
                    TargetPlayer = Game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(RaycastTarget.Parent)
                elseif RaycastTarget.Parent:IsA("Accessory") then
                    TargetPlayer = Game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(RaycastTarget.Parent.Parent)
                end
                if TargetPlayer then
                    UpdateTarget(TargetPlayer)
                end
            end
        end
        ClickTool.Activated:Connect(function()
            HandleClickActivation()
        end)
        ClickTool.Parent = LocalPlayer.Backpack
    end)
    FlingTargetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            ChangeToggleColor(FlingTargetButton)
            ViewTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FocusTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            HeadsitTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            StandTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            BackpackTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            if FlingTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
                Game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
                    Title = "System VR7",
                    Text = "\239\191\189\216\176\216\167 \217\133\216\167\216\183\216\167\216\177 \216\167\217\132\216\167\216\185\216\168 \217\133\216\185\217\134\216\167\217\135\216\167 \216\167\217\132\217\133\216\167\216\168 \217\129\217\138\217\135 \216\173\217\133\216\167\217\138\216\169",
                    Duration = 3
                })
                if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and (Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid and Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart) then
                    if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude < 50 then
                        Getgenv().OldPos = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.CFrame
                    end
                    if PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Head then
                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Head
                    elseif PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Accessory"):FindFirstChild("Handle") then
                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Accessory"):FindFirstChild("Handle")
                    else
                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid
                    end
                    if not PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("BasePart") then
                        return
                    end
                    local function TeleportPlayer(RootPart, PositionOffset, RotationCFrame)
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(RootPart.Position) * PositionOffset * RotationCFrame
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame.New(RootPart.Position) * PositionOffset * RotationCFrame)
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity = Vector3.New(90000000, 900000000, 90000000)
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.New(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
                    end
                    local function ToggleAntiFling()
                        Getgenv().FPDH = Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight
                        Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
                        local HeightIncrement = 0
                        repeat
                            Task.Wait()
                            Pcall(function()
                                if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart and PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid then
                                    if PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude >= 50 then
                                        local IteratorFunction, TableToIterate, CurrentIndex = Ipairs({
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, 1.5, PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed),
                                                Math.Rad(90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, - PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed),
                                                0
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, 1.5, PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed),
                                                Math.Rad(90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, 1.5, PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.25),
                                                Math.Rad(90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, - PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.25),
                                                0
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, 1.5, PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.25),
                                                Math.Rad(90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0),
                                                Math.Rad(90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0),
                                                0
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0),
                                                Math.Rad(- 90)
                                            },
                                            {
                                                Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0),
                                                0
                                            }
                                        })
                                        while true do
                                            local CurrentValue
                                            CurrentIndex, CurrentValue = IteratorFunction(TableToIterate, CurrentIndex)
                                            if CurrentIndex == nil then
                                                break
                                            end
                                            TeleportPlayer(PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart, CFrame.New(CurrentValue[1]), CFrame.Angles(CurrentValue[2], 0, 0))
                                            Task.Wait()
                                        end
                                    else
                                        HeightIncrement = HeightIncrement + 100
                                        local VectorIteratorFunction, VectorTableToIterate, CurrentIndex = Ipairs({
                                            Vector3.New(0, 1.5, 0),
                                            Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0),
                                            Vector3.New(2.25, 1.5, - 2.25),
                                            Vector3.New(- 2.25, - 1.5, 2.25),
                                            Vector3.New(0, 1.5, 0),
                                            Vector3.New(0, - 1.5, 0)
                                        })
                                        while true do
                                            local CurrentValue
                                            CurrentIndex, CurrentValue = VectorIteratorFunction(VectorTableToIterate, CurrentIndex)
                                            if CurrentIndex == nil then
                                                break
                                            end
                                            TeleportPlayer(PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart, CFrame.New(CurrentValue) + PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.MoveDirection * (PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.25), CFrame.Angles(Math.Rad(HeightIncrement), 0, 0))
                                            Task.Wait()
                                        end
                                    end
                                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                                    if PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character:FindFirstChild("Head") then
                                        Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Head
                                    end
                                end
                            end)
                        until FlingTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0)
                    end
                    local FlingerBodyVelocity = Instance.New("BodyVelocity")
                    FlingerBodyVelocity.Name = "Flinger"
                    FlingerBodyVelocity.Parent = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart
                    FlingerBodyVelocity.Velocity = Vector3.New(900000000, 900000000, 900000000)
                    FlingerBodyVelocity.MaxForce = Vector3.New(1 / 0, 1 / 0, 1 / 0)
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, false)
                    ToggleAntiFling()
                    FlingerBodyVelocity:Destroy()
                    Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:SetStateEnabled(Enum.HumanoidStateType.Seated, true)
                    Workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid
                    repeat
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.CFrame = Getgenv().OldPos * CFrame.New(0, 0.5, 0)
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(Getgenv().OldPos * CFrame.New(0, 0.5, 0))
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState("GettingUp")
                        Table.Foreach(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:GetChildren(), function(_, CharacterPart)
                            if CharacterPart:IsA("BasePart") then
                                local ZeroVector = Vector3.New()
                                CharacterPart.RotVelocity = Vector3.New()
                                CharacterPart.Velocity = ZeroVector
                            end
                        end)
                        Task.Wait()
                    until (Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RootPart.Position - Getgenv().OldPos.Position).Magnitude < 25
                    Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = Getgenv().FPDH
                    if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit then
                        Wait(1)
                        Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end)

                    if ChatMessage.TextSource and ChatMessage.TextSource.UserId == PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].UserId then
                        Task.Wait(0.001)
                        local HttpRequest = Request
                        local RequestOptions = {
                            Url = "https://roblox-aiii.vercel.app/api/chat",
                            Method = "POST",
                            Headers = {
                                ["Content-Type"] = "application/json"
                            },
                            Body = HttpService:JSONEncode({
                                Question = Tostring(ChatMessage.Text)
                            })
                        }
                        local HttpResponse = HttpRequest(RequestOptions)
                        Send(Game:GetService("HttpService"):JSONDecode(HttpResponse.Body).Response)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end)

        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            ChangeToggleColor(StandTargetButton)
            ViewTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FocusTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)

            FlingTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            HeadsitTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            BackpackTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            if StandTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
                local PlayerIterator, PlayerList, CurrentPlayer = Pairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks())
                while true do
                    local LoopControl
                    CurrentPlayer, LoopControl = PlayerIterator(PlayerList, CurrentPlayer)
                    if CurrentPlayer == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    LoopControl:Stop()
                end
                local SitOffset = - 2
                local OffsetIncrement = 0.3
                repeat
                    Task.Wait(0.01)
                    Pcall(function()
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Parent.Humanoid.Sit = true
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].Character.Head.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 0.7, SitOffset) * CFrame.Angles(0, Math.Rad(180), 0)
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0, 0)
                        SitOffset = SitOffset + OffsetIncrement
                        if SitOffset >= - 1 or SitOffset <= - 2 then
                            OffsetIncrement = - OffsetIncrement
                        end
                    end)
                until StandTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Parent.Humanoid.Sit = false
            end
        end
    end)
    BackpackTargetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            ChangeToggleColor(BackpackTargetButton)
            ViewTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FocusTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FlingTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            HeadsitTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            StandTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            if BackpackTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
                repeat
                    Pcall(function()
                        local TargetRootPart = GetRoot(PlayersService[TargetPlayerName])
                        LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = true
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = TargetRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 0, 1.2) * CFrame.Angles(0, - 3, 0)
                        GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0, 0)
                    end)
                    Task.Wait()
                until BackpackTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Parent.Humanoid.Sit = false
            end
        end
    end)
    TargetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            ChangeToggleColor(TargetButton)
            ViewTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FocusTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            FlingTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            HeadsitTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            StandTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            BackpackTargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            if TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
                Spawn(function()
                    Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
                    while TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) do
                        Pcall(function()
                            if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                                if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RigType ~= Enum.HumanoidRigType.RigTypeR6 then
                                    if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.IsR15RigType then
                                        PlayAnim(698251653, 0.6, 0.4, true)
                                        Task.Wait(0.16)
                                    end
                                else
                                    PlayAnim(72042024, 0.675, 1, true)
                                    Wait(0.4)
                                end
                            end
                        end)
                        Task.Wait()
                    end
                    StopAnim()
                end)
                repeat
                    Pcall(function()
                        if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
                            local TargetRootPart = GetRoot(PlayersService[TargetPlayerName])
                            Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:ChangeState("GettingUp")
                            if not Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit then
                                Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = true
                            end
                            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).CFrame = TargetRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.New(0, 1, - 3) * CFrame.Angles(0, Math.PiConstant, 0)
                            GetRoot(LocalPlayer).Velocity = Vector3.New(0, 0, 0)
                        end
                    end)
                    Task.Wait()
                until TargetButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
                Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = - 500
                Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false
            end
        end
    end)
    RepeatTalkButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            ChangeToggleColor(RepeatTalkButton)
            if RepeatTalkButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
                if TalkRepeater then
                    TalkRepeater:Disconnect()
                end
            else
                TalkRepeater = Game:GetService("TextChatService").MessageReceived:Connect(function(ChatMessage)
                    if ChatMessage.TextSource and ChatMessage.TextSource.UserId == PlayersService[TargetPlayerName].UserId then
                        Send(ChatMessage.Text)
                    end
                end)
            end
        end
    end)
    TeleportTargetButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if TargetPlayerName ~= nil then
            TeleportTO(0, 0, 0, PlayersService[TargetPlayerName], nil)
        end
    end)
    TargetNameInput.FocusLost:Connect(function()
        local TargetPlayerName = FindPlayerByName(TargetNameInput.Text)
        UpdateTarget(TargetPlayerName)
    end)

    getgenv().CrazyAnimationR15.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.IsR15RigType then
            Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = false
            local CustomAnimation = Instance.New("Animation")
            CustomAnimation.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://10713957138"
            local AnimationIterator, AnimationTrack, CurrentAnimation = Pairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks())
            while true do
                local PlayingAnimationTrack
                CurrentAnimation, PlayingAnimationTrack = AnimationIterator(AnimationTrack, CurrentAnimation)
                if CurrentAnimation == nil then
                    break
                end
                if PlayingAnimationTrack.Animation.AnimationId ~= CustomAnimation.AnimationId then
                    PlayingAnimationTrack:Stop()
                else
                    PlayingAnimationTrack:Stop()
                    Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = true
                end
            end
            if Getgenv().Idkjustcheck then
                Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = false
            else
                local LoadedAnimation = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid"):LoadAnimation(CustomAnimation)
                LoadedAnimation.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action
                LoadedAnimation.Looped = true
                LoadedAnimation:Play()
                LoadedAnimation:AdjustSpeed(4)
            end
        else
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\172\216\168 \216\167\217\134 \216\170\217\131\217\136\217\134 R15", 7)
            return
        end
    end)

    getgenv().JerkingAnimationButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.RigType == Enum.HumanoidRigType.RigTypeR6 then
            Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = false
            local DanceAnimation1 = Instance.New("Animation")
            DanceAnimation1.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://204292303"
            local DanceAnimation2 = Instance.New("Animation")
            DanceAnimation2.AnimationId = "rbxassetid://181526230"
            local AnimationIterator, AnimationTable, CurrentAnimationTrack = Pairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid:GetPlayingAnimationTracks())
            while true do
                local AnimationTrack
                CurrentAnimationTrack, AnimationTrack = AnimationIterator(AnimationTable, CurrentAnimationTrack)
                if CurrentAnimationTrack == nil then
                    break
                end
                if AnimationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == DanceAnimation1.AnimationId or AnimationTrack.Animation.AnimationId == DanceAnimation2.AnimationId then
                    AnimationTrack:Stop()
                    Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = true
                else
                    AnimationTrack:Stop()
                end
            end
            if Getgenv().Idkjustcheck then
                Getgenv().Idkjustcheck = false
            else
                local Humanoid = Game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")
                local AnimationTrack1 = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(DanceAnimation1)
                AnimationTrack1.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action
                AnimationTrack1.Looped = true
                AnimationTrack1:Play(0.1, 1, 3)
                Track1 = Humanoid:LoadAnimation(DanceAnimation2)
                Track1.Priority = Enum.AnimationPriority.Action
                Track1.Looped = true
                Track1:Play(0.1, 1, 1)
            end
        else
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\216\172\216\168 \216\167\217\134 \216\170\217\131\217\136\217\134 R6", 7)
            return
        end
    end)

    AntiFlingButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(AntiFlingButton)
        if AntiFlingButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            _G.AntiFlingToggled = false
        else
            _G.AntiFlingToggled = true
            Loadstring(Game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/H20CalibreYT/SystemBroken/main/AntiFling"))()
        end
    end)
    local IsGettingUp = false
    AntiChatSpyButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(AntiChatSpyButton)
        if AntiChatSpyButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            SendNotify("System VR7", "\239\191\189\217\134 \216\167\217\132\217\133\217\133\217\131\217\134 \216\167\217\132\217\133\216\182\216\167\216\175 \217\133\216\167\217\138\217\131\216\180\217\129 \216\168\216\185\216\182 \216\167\217\134\217\136\216\167\216\185 \216\179\217\131\216\177\216\168\216\170\216\167\216\170 \216\167\217\132\216\167\216\186\216\170\216\181\216\167\216\168", 7)
            repeat
                Pcall(function()
                    Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = 0 / 0
                    Character = LocalPlayer.Character
                    local HumanoidInstance = Character
                    if HumanoidInstance then
                        HumanoidInstance = Character:FindFirstChildWhichIsA("Humanoid")
                    end
                    Humanoid = HumanoidInstance
                    local RootPart = Humanoid
                    if RootPart then
                        RootPart = Humanoid.RootPart
                    end
                    RootPart = RootPart
                    if IsRootPartValid() and (Humanoid and (RootPart and not IsGettingUp)) then
                        IsGettingUp = true
                        local TargetCFrame = RootPart.Velocity.Magnitude < 50 and RootPart.CFrame or CurrentCamera.Focus
                        local AntiFlingStartTime = Tick()
                        repeat
                            RootPart.CFrame = CFrame.New(0, - 499, 0) * CFrame.Angles(Math.Rad(90), 0, 0)
                            RootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.New()
                            Task.Wait()
                        until Tick() > AntiFlingStartTime + 1
                        RootPart.AssemblyLinearVelocity = Vector3.New()
                        RootPart.CFrame = TargetCFrame
                        Humanoid:ChangeState(Enum.HumanoidStateType.GettingUp)
                        IsGettingUp = false
                    end
                end)
                Task.Wait()
            until AntiChatSpyButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor == Color3.FromRGB(255, 0, 0)
            Workspace.FallenPartsDestroyHeight = - 500
        end
    end)
    local IdleConnection = nil
    AntiAFKButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(AntiAFKButton)
        if AntiAFKButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            IdleConnection:Disconnect()
        else
            IdleConnection = LocalPlayer.Idled:Connect(function()
                local VirtualUserService = Game:GetService("VirtualUser")
                VirtualUserService:CaptureController()
                VirtualUserService:ClickButton2(Vector2.New())
            end)
        end
    end)
    ShadersButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        ChangeToggleColor(ShadersButton)
        if ShadersButton.Ticket_Asset.ToggleIndicatorColor ~= Color3.FromRGB(0, 255, 0) then
            local ChildrenCollection = LightingService
            local IteratorFunction, ChildTable, CurrentIndex = Pairs(ChildrenCollection:GetChildren())
            while true do
                local CurrentChild
                CurrentIndex, CurrentChild = IteratorFunction(ChildTable, CurrentIndex)
                if CurrentIndex == nil then
                    break
                end
                CurrentChild:Destroy()
            end
            LightingService.Brightness = 2
            LightingService.ExposureCompensation = 0
        else
            local SkyInstance = Instance.New("Sky")
            local BloomEffectInstance = Instance.New("BloomEffect")
            local BlurEffectInstance = Instance.New("BlurEffect")
            local ColorCorrectionInstance = Instance.New("ColorCorrectionEffect")
            local SunRaysEffect = Instance.New("SunRaysEffect")
            LightingService.Brightness = 2.25
            LightingService.ExposureCompensation = 0.1
            LightingService.ClockTime = 17.55
            SkyInstance.SkyboxBk = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144933338"
            SkyInstance.SkyboxDn = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144931530"
            SkyInstance.SkyboxFt = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144933262"
            SkyInstance.SkyboxLf = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144933244"
            SkyInstance.SkyboxRt = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144933299"
            SkyInstance.SkyboxUp = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=144931564"
            SkyInstance.StarCount = 5000
            SkyInstance.SunAngularSize = 5
            SkyInstance.Parent = LightingService
            BloomEffectInstance.Intensity = 0.3
            BloomEffectInstance.Size = 10
            BloomEffectInstance.Threshold = 0.8
            BloomEffectInstance.Parent = LightingService
            BlurEffectInstance.Size = 5
            BlurEffectInstance.Parent = LightingService
            ColorCorrectionInstance.Brightness = 0
            ColorCorrectionInstance.Contrast = 0.1
            ColorCorrectionInstance.Saturation = 0.25
            ColorCorrectionInstance.TintColor = Color3.FromRGB(255, 255, 255)
            ColorCorrectionInstance.Parent = LightingService
            SunRaysEffect.Intensity = 0.1
            SunRaysEffect.Spread = 0.8
            SunRaysEffect.Parent = LightingService
        end
    end)

    ServerHopButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        if QueueOnTeleport then
            QueueOnTeleport("loadstring(game:HttpGet(\"https://raw.githubusercontent.com/VR7ss/OMK/refs/heads/main/VR7-ON-TOP\"))()")
        end
        local TeleportSettings = {
            MaxStore = 3600,
            CheckInterval = 1,
            TeleportInterval = 1
        }
        local HttpService = Game:GetService("HttpService")
        local TeleportService = Game:GetService("TeleportService")
        local LocalPlayer = Game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
        local PlaceId = Game.PlaceId
        local JobId = Game.JobId
        local ServerHopFolderName = "ServerHop"
        local ServerDataFilePath = String.Format("%s\\%s.json", ServerHopFolderName, Tostring(PlaceId))
        local DefaultServerData = {
            Start = Tick(),
            Jobs = {}
        }
        if not Isfolder(ServerHopFolderName) then
            Makefolder(ServerHopFolderName)
        end
        local StoredServerData
        if Isfile(ServerDataFilePath) then
            StoredServerData = HttpService:JSONDecode(Readfile(ServerDataFilePath))
            if Tick() - StoredServerData.Start >= TeleportSettings.MaxStore then
                StoredServerData = DefaultServerData
            end
        else
            StoredServerData = DefaultServerData
        end
        if not Table.Find(StoredServerData.Jobs, JobId) then
            Table.Insert(StoredServerData.Jobs, JobId)
        end
        Writefile(ServerDataFilePath, HttpService:JSONEncode(StoredServerData))
        local NextPageCursor = ""
        local ServerInstances = {}
        while NextPageCursor and (# ServerInstances <= 0 and Task.Wait(TeleportSettings.CheckInterval / 1000)) do
            local HttpResponse = (Request or HttpService.RequestAsync)({
                Url = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Desc&limit=100&excludeFullGames=true&cursor=" .. NextPageCursor,
                Method = "GET"
            })
            local DecodeSuccess, DecodedData = Pcall(function()
                return HttpService:JSONDecode(HttpResponse.Body)
            end)
            if not (DecodeSuccess and (DecodedData and DecodedData.Data)) then
                break
            end
            local DataIterator, CurrentKey, CurrentValue = Pairs(DecodedData.Data)
            while true do
                local ServerData
                CurrentValue, ServerData = DataIterator(CurrentKey, CurrentValue)
                if CurrentValue == nil then
                    break
                end
                if Typeof(ServerData) == "table" and (ServerData.ServerId and (Tonumber(ServerData.Playing) and (Tonumber(ServerData.MaxPlayers) and (ServerData.Playing < ServerData.MaxPlayers and not Table.Find(StoredServerData.Jobs, ServerData.ServerId))))) then
                    Table.Insert(ServerInstances, 1, ServerData.ServerId)
                end
            end
            NextPageCursor = DecodedData.NextPageCursor or nil
        end
        while # ServerInstances > 0 and Task.Wait(TeleportSettings.TeleportInterval / 1000) do
            TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(PlaceId, ServerInstances[Math.Random(1, # ServerInstances)], LocalPlayer)
        end
    end)

    WhoWeAreButton.MouseButton1Click:Connect(function()
        local LocalPlayer = Game.Players.LocalPlayer
        local ScreenGuiInstance = Instance.New("ScreenGui", LocalPlayer:WaitForChild("PlayerGui"))
        ScreenGuiInstance.ResetOnSpawn = false
        ScreenGuiInstance.IgnoreGuiInset = true
        local CoreGuiDescendantsIterator, CoreGuiDescendantsTable, CurrentDescendantKey = Pairs(Game.CoreGui:GetDescendants())
        local DisabledScreens = {}
        while true do
            local CurrentDescendant
            CurrentDescendantKey, CurrentDescendant = CoreGuiDescendantsIterator(CoreGuiDescendantsTable, CurrentDescendantKey)
            if CurrentDescendantKey == nil then
                break
            end
            if CurrentDescendant:IsA("ScreenGui") and (CurrentDescendant ~= ScreenGuiInstance and CurrentDescendant.Enabled) then
                Table.Insert(DisabledScreens, CurrentDescendant)
                CurrentDescendant.Enabled = false
            end
        end
        local DescendantsIterator, DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant = Pairs(Game.Players.LocalPlayer.PlayerGui:GetDescendants())
        while true do
            local DescendantInstance
            CurrentDescendant, DescendantInstance = DescendantsIterator(DescendantsTable, CurrentDescendant)
            if CurrentDescendant == nil then
                break
            end
            if DescendantInstance:IsA("ScreenGui") and (DescendantInstance ~= ScreenGuiInstance and DescendantInstance.Enabled) then
                Table.Insert(DisabledScreens, DescendantInstance)
                DescendantInstance.Enabled = false
            end
        end
        local MainFrame = Instance.New("Frame", ScreenGuiInstance)
        MainFrame.Size = UDim2.New(1, 0, 1, 0)
        MainFrame.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(0, 0, 0)
        MainFrame.BorderSizePixel = 0
        MainFrame.ZIndex = 10
        local ContentLabel = Instance.New("TextLabel", MainFrame)
        ContentLabel.Size = UDim2.New(0.8, 0, 0.6, 0)
        ContentLabel.Position = UDim2.New(0.1, 0, 0.2, 0)
        ContentLabel.Text = Loadstring(Game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Hm5011/hussain/refs/heads/main/Warn%20Message"))()
        ContentLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(PrimaryColorR, GreenComponent, BlueComponent)
        ContentLabel.TextScaled = true
        ContentLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        ContentLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
        ContentLabel.TextWrapped = true
        ContentLabel.ZIndex = 11
        local CountdownLabel = Instance.New("TextLabel", MainFrame)
        CountdownLabel.Size = UDim2.New(0.2, 0, 0.1, 0)
        CountdownLabel.Position = UDim2.New(0.05, 0, 0.85, 0)
        CountdownLabel.TextColor3 = Color3.FromRGB(PrimaryColorR, GreenComponent, BlueComponent)
        CountdownLabel.TextScaled = true
        CountdownLabel.BackgroundTransparency = 1
        CountdownLabel.Font = Enum.Font.SourceSansBold
        CountdownLabel.Text = "20"
        CountdownLabel.ZIndex = 12
        for CountdownValue = 20, 0, - 1 do
            CountdownLabel.Text = Tostring(CountdownValue)
            Wait(1)
        end
        Pcall(function()
            ScreenGuiInstance:Destroy()
            local IteratorFunction, TableState, CurrentKey = Pairs(DisabledScreens)
            while true do
                local CurrentValue
                CurrentKey, CurrentValue = IteratorFunction(TableState, CurrentKey)
                if CurrentKey == nil then
                    break
                end
                CurrentValue.Enabled = true
            end
        end)
    end)
